British Representative Reviews World Situation, Sternly Condemns Soviet Attitude, Hopes Soviet Union Will Change Course and Save Peace

[This newspaper's dispatch] Broadcast from Lake Success on the 22nd: Today, British Minister of State Mr. McNeil, the chief representative attending the United Nations General Assembly, delivered a speech to the assembly, 2,600 words long, clarifying the basic policies of the United Kingdom. It stated that if the Soviet Union continues to force its will upon the countries of the world, world peace will collapse, causing serious consequences. He criticized the Soviet Union sternly, but still hoped that the Soviet Union would change its attitude. Mr. McNeil dismissed as absurd Vyshinsky's claim that the United States has a tendency to instigate war. He strongly denied Vyshinsky's claim that the Marshall Plan for European economic aid threatens the sovereignty of European countries, and pointed out that the Soviet Union deliberately hindered the passage of the atomic energy control plan and used its veto power ten times. Mr. McNeil's speech touched on all aspects of the world political situation, but his main argument was to condemn the Soviet Union's uncompromising attitude and the serious impact of this attitude on world peace. Mr. McNeil also said that the Four-Power Foreign Ministers Conference to be held in London in November this year will be the last hope for restoring peace.

[United Press, Flushing Meadow, 22nd] Britain today joined the United States in publicly criticizing the Soviet Union for undermining the United Nations. Austin, in his first official reply to the Soviet Union, bluntly accused Vyshinsky of lying by calling the United States a "war monger," and said that Vyshinsky's speech at the General Assembly was a slanderous and provocative lie. British representative McNeil, following Austin's lead, will deliver a speech at the General Assembly to "shatter" the Soviet Union's arguments accusing Britain and the United States of being war mongers and undermining the United Nations. Mr. McNeil will review the entire situation of the United Nations, and, like Marshall, will completely blame the Soviet Union for the current paralysis.

Amendment to the Italian Peace Treaty Added to UN General Assembly Agenda, China, Britain and Other Allied Nations Abstain, Soviet Union and Poland Vote Against

[Reuters, Lake Success, New York, 21st] The Steering Committee of the General Assembly today passed by a vote of four to two to add the amendment to the Italian Peace Treaty to the agenda for discussion by the General Assembly. The United States, Mexico, Cuba, and Brazil voted in favor, and the Soviet Union and Poland voted against. Eight countries, including China and Britain, abstained. The proposal was put forward by Argentina. British representative Shawcross said during the discussion that the British government believes that it is unwise for the General Assembly to discuss the amendment of the Italian Peace Treaty at this time. The British government has always believed that the provisions of the Italian Peace Treaty are not entirely satisfactory, but it is very doubtful whether it is appropriate to amend it at this time. Although the United Kingdom does not oppose the proposal, it does not seem to be able to support it. Polish representative Ransan Lian told the meeting that the General Assembly's immediate discussion of the amendment to the Italian Peace Treaty would dangerously hinder the conclusion of peace treaties with Germany and Japan. The Allied countries would therefore allow Germany and Japan to sign peace treaties with extremely strong reservations. The Italian Peace Treaty has only been ratified for one week, and the General Assembly's discussion of its amendment is a great encouragement to Germany and Japan. Syrian representative Koli advocated that the Security Council should quickly recommend Italy's accession to the United Nations. After joining, Italy would have the opportunity to request an amendment to the treaty. Soviet representative Gromyko said that the United States did not express any intention to amend the treaty when negotiating the Italian Peace Treaty, and the United States' sudden change of attitude did not surprise the Soviet Union. This move by the United States would make it impossible for the Allied countries to cooperate more easily when negotiating peace treaties with Germany and Japan. Argentina's proposal suggested that countries that signed the Italian Peace Treaty should give Italy the opportunity to put forward new opinions to reduce the obligations imposed on Italy by the treaty.

Steering Committee Passes Soviet Proposal to Add to Agenda

[Central News Agency, Flushing, 21st] After clarifying that the General Assembly has full authority to discuss any issues related to international security and peace, the Steering Committee of the General Assembly today unanimously passed the Soviet proposal to add to the agenda the case of the General Assembly adopting countermeasures to stop the propaganda and instigation of another war.

[Associated Press dispatch] The Steering Committee then quickly passed two Yugoslav proposals with the following content: To prevent the dissemination of defamatory reports against foreign countries, so as to harm international friendship and violate the purposes and principles of the United Nations organization. To ensure the extradition of war criminals, traitors and puppets to the victimized countries.

British Colonial Secretary Jones Flies to New York to Attend Discussion on Palestine Issue

[Reuters, London, 22nd] British Colonial Secretary Jones is scheduled to fly to New York today to attend the General Assembly meeting and present Britain's views during the debate on the Palestine issue. The British government's position has been decided by the cabinet at a special meeting on Friday. It is expected that Jones will declare that if the United Nations organization has no new proposals, Britain is prepared to hand over the trusteeship of the Holy Land and withdraw its troops from the area.

[Associated Press, London, 21st] Foreign Office officials declared today: After Britain submitted the Palestine issue to the General Assembly, it is willing to accept the partition plan for Palestine, but will insist that other member states assist in fulfilling this task. This point is recognized as the future position of the British government.

[Associated Press, London, 21st] The Arab League representative declared today: If the United Nations wants to partition Palestine, the Arab countries will implement economic and cultural sanctions against Europe and the United States.

British Foreign Office Spokesman Criticizes Romanian and Bulgarian Governments, Also Issues Warning to Hungary

[Central News Agency, London, 21st, United Press] A British Foreign Office spokesman today criticized the Bulgarian and Romanian governments for not being able to represent their countries, saying that if these countries violate the principles of the peace treaty again, they will constitute a crime against European civilization. His attack on Hungary was lighter, believing that there were many Communists in the country and their power was disproportionate, and said, "The lessons of Romania and Bulgaria should be a warning to the Hungarians."

France Willing to Act as Mediator to Eliminate Differences Between the United States and the Soviet Union, President and Prime Minister Call for Peace in Speeches

[Reuters, Paris, 21st] Since Marshall and Vyshinsky had a head-on conflict at the General Assembly meeting, French people have been fearing that a new war will break out again. The words of French President Auriol and Prime Minister Ramadier also reflect this mentality. Both of them stressed that France will continue to work hard to reconcile the opinions of the East and the West. They also declared that the peace treaty with Germany should ensure that France has security guarantees, and France should have preferential rights over Germany in economic reconstruction. Auriol said that he earnestly hopes that the powerful countries guiding world affairs can assume the highest responsibility and bring peace to the world. If peace cannot be achieved among the powerful countries, and the armed fear that will inevitably lead to war continues to be maintained, it will be a terrible mockery of the fate of mankind. Prime Minister Ramadier also said that Europe does not exclude any country, and recognizes that both the Soviet Union and the United Kingdom are part of Europe. The table in Europe is a round table, which allows all countries in Eastern and Western Europe to sit at the same table in a completely equal position. He continued, the foundation of peace is now threatened, and if peace is not guaranteed, nothing will be achieved. The diverse interpretations within the country caused by French Foreign Minister Bidault's speech at the General Assembly reflect the fact that most of the French people are unwilling to be forced to definitely participate in the ranks of either the Soviet Union or the Soviet Union.

Indonesian Government Announces Basic Policy Towards the Netherlands, Foreign Minister Wang Meets With Sjahrir

[Reuters, Batavia, 22nd] Radio Yogyakarta announced: The Indonesian cabinet held a meeting for three days under the chairmanship of President Sukarno, and announced on the night of the 22nd the basic policy of the Republic towards the Netherlands, the main points of which are as follows: The Indonesian cabinet has decided to eliminate the unrest and disorder caused by the Dutch military's invasion of Indonesian territory; The cabinet is determined to maintain peace and order, as well as the freedom of action of the Indonesian people; Post-war reconstruction work on the islands will continue, regardless of whether there is assistance from the Dutch side; Foreign relations will be strengthened.

According to a spokesman for the Republic, the Republic will use these points as a standard to cooperate with the rest of the world on the basis of equality. If the Dutch are willing to accept the above promises, peace talks can begin immediately. This conflict was initiated by the Dutch side, and the Indonesian government has no intention of continuing the state of conflict. The spokesman also said that before peace negotiations begin, the Dutch military must withdraw from the territory occupied by its so-called police action. The Indonesian army is prepared to take over as soon as the Dutch military withdraws.

[Central News Agency, New York, 21st] Former Indonesian Prime Minister Sjahrir visited Foreign Minister Wang Shijie today. It is learned that Foreign Minister Ren Wang reiterated during the half-hour conversation the Chinese policy of following Dr. Sun Yat-sen's principle of Asian independence. Wang emphasized to Sjahrir the necessity for the Indonesian Republic to provide effective protection for the lives and property of overseas Chinese within its borders. Sjahrir will go to London tonight, and then to Singapore, before returning to Java. His planned trip to Nanjing was cancelled after he visited Foreign Minister Wang today.

[Associated Press, Batavia, 22nd] The United Nations Consular Investigation Team issued a communiqué today, stating that the team has decided to immediately submit an interim report to the Security Council on the supervision of the implementation of the ceasefire order by the Dutch and Indonesia, and hopes to complete its work around the end of September.

Truman and Cabinet Members Begin Consultations, Marshall Returns to Washington Posthaste, Opinions Differ on Convening Special Session of Congress

[United Press, Washington, 22nd] President Truman held a meeting with three cabinet members today to discuss the two urgent issues of increasing aid to Europe and balancing domestic prices.

[Associated Press, Washington, 21st] Secretary of State Marshall took time out from New York tonight to return here to meet with President Truman tomorrow afternoon to discuss world political and economic issues and decide on countermeasures for major issues.

[Associated Press, Washington, 21st] President Truman discovered on the 21st that his senior advisers had sharp divisions of opinion on current serious issues, namely whether to convene a special session of Congress to deal with the increasingly serious domestic and foreign economic crises. Administration officials said that the president would be forced to reach a "gentleman's agreement" with Republican congressional leaders before taking any action. For this reason, Truman's subordinates are all strongly opposed to convening a special session of Congress unless it is a last resort. It is said that the authorities suggested that the Republican-controlled Congress is very likely to reject the group leader to stop the high domestic prices and the European famine problem. On the other hand, the Secretary of State expressed that this emergency action is necessary to save Europe. If the Congress of the War is not convened, the necessary expedient aid policy cannot be implemented.

Economic Conference of 16 European Countries, Representatives Sign Report, Needs US Aid of $16 Billion

[Associated Press, Paris, 22nd] The Economic Cooperation Conference of 16 European countries has been held for ten weeks. This afternoon, representatives went to the French Ministry of Foreign Affairs to sign the report, which is 20,000 words long. It lists the resources, self-help procedures of Western and Southern Europe, and, based on the needs of US Secretary of State Marshall's plan for European economic recovery, suggests that the United States should provide aid of $16.295 billion in the next four years. A British Air Force special plane is now on standby to transport the report to Washington. According to people attending the meeting, the budget for income and expenditure from 1948 to 1951 is as follows: The 16 European countries must import food, raw materials, and production equipment totaling $35 billion. $15 billion can be offset by exports or other means. The shortage totals $19.689 billion, of which $3.394 billion will be borrowed from the International Bank for Reconstruction and Development, and the remaining $16.295 billion should be provided by the United States. All representatives are uneasy about the outcome of the report. The final decision on this matter rests with the US Congress, and the US Congress may not be able to discuss it until next spring, but it is hoped that the United States can design temporary aid measures.

Egypt to Expand Military, Workers Hold Anti-British and American Demonstrations

[Reuters, Cairo, 21st] Egyptian Prime Minister Nokrashy addressed the Saadi Party he founded after returning to the country from the United States yesterday, saying that Egypt's top priority at present is to strengthen its military strength to cope with any contingencies. Soviet Union Incapable of War in Next 25 Years, Observations of Mr. Reppsche

[United Press, Washington, 21st] Mr. Reppsche, director of the Soviet Union Department of the State Department, told reporters today that the Soviet Union's industry is incapable of preparing for war against the United States for at least 25 years. This weakness may extend to 50 years, and we do not need to worry about the Soviet Union as a potential enemy. Mr. Reppsche has been studying the Soviet Union for 24 years and said that the Soviet Union is using all its strength to build heavy industry, especially steel, railways, and farm implements. Light industry accounts for only one-third of its post-war recovery plan. Mr. Reppsche did not mention how the Soviet Union's satellite countries and the Soviet-occupied zone of Germany supply the Soviet Union.

Some US Officials Stationed in Japan Advocate That Japan Should Have a Large-Scale Merchant Fleet, Claimed That the Minimum Livelihood of the Japanese Cannot Be Maintained Without This

[United Press, Tokyo, 22nd] Several US officials here said that Japan should be allowed to have a fairly large-scale merchant fleet to achieve the living standards stipulated by the Allied countries. Japan itself cannot produce enough products and cannot obtain goods from foreign countries. Therefore, if Japan needs to achieve the minimum standard of living, it should have a good merchant fleet. An Allied official said: "If Japan can have a merchant fleet, it can increase its national income and make up for the shortcomings that exist between its necessities and the gains from its small export trade." If Japan encourages travel and trade to Japan, operates a "merchant fleet," and transports raw materials from abroad, it can establish its foreign assets. An Allied official said that Japan currently has 777 iron-hulled ships of more than 100 tons, with a total tonnage of more than one million tons. In 1939, Japan had a total tonnage of 5,629,845 tons. Since 1927, the tonnage of Japanese ships has been more than 4 million tons.

Iranian Parliament Opens Fierce Debate on Transfer of Oil Rights to Soviet Union, Opposition Party Accuses Negotiations of Being Illegal

This move attempts to encourage buyers to purchase more Japanese goods and to provide Japanese exporters with a better opportunity to compete in the world market.

Fourth Session of the Municipal Council Opens – Speaker Presents Three Points – Austerity Movement Has Reached an Inevitable Stage

(Our Report) The fourth session of the first Shanghai Municipal Council officially opened at 9:00 AM yesterday at the Council's location on Tanggu Road. 146 councilors were in attendance, with Mayor Wu, bureau chiefs, and other party, government, and military leaders, along with chairmen of district people's representative assemblies, district保長 (bao zhang, local heads), and dozens of others present as observers. At the opening ceremony, Speaker Pan delivered a speech, stating: "The first general assembly of the Shanghai Municipal Council was held in September of last year, and a year has now passed. In the past year, although we have not made many suggestions and contributions to municipal facilities, we have more or less fulfilled our responsibility to represent the citizens, increase their welfare, and reduce their suffering. At the same time, we have also considered the needs of the municipal government, hoping to do as much as possible under poor economic conditions." The speaker also mentioned that the current situation is at a critical juncture, and that the high prices in the city are related to the overall situation. The Mid-Autumn Festival is also approaching, and prices tend to fluctuate during this period. Therefore, this session is also very important. Although the session is short, we must do our best to contribute our opinions on local political and social trends, as well as the overall national situation.

Finally, he put forward three suggestions based on his personal thoughts: "The municipal government's budget for the 37th year of the Republic [1948] must be submitted during this session. If we wait until the next session in December, it will be too late to submit it to the central government for approval. Therefore, we hope that the municipal government will expedite the preparation of the budget for the next year without increasing the burden on citizens or hindering the work of the municipal government. The council should also review it as soon as possible. The austerity movement should be actively promoted. Looking at the current situation in Shanghai, it is a great crisis. The four supervisory committee members who came to Shanghai to investigate last time expressed their feeling that the extravagance of a few people in Shanghai caused the majority to be unable to live. This statement is worth paying attention to. At the same time, Shanghai is an international city, and foreigners coming to Shanghai often express that China is asking for loans from foreign countries, so why not raise funds from the people of Shanghai themselves? Therefore, the austerity movement has reached a stage where it must be implemented. The central government has not yet determined the status of municipalities directly under the central government. The constitution only states that the autonomy of municipalities directly under the central government will be "separately defined by law." Therefore, we hope that the council will study the autonomous status of municipalities directly under the central government as much as possible and contribute to the central government based on Shanghai's past experience in local autonomy." In addition, he also reported that, as a result of the joint efforts of the municipal government and the council, the central government has given satisfactory answers to the return of enemy and puppet-occupied civil land and property and the organization of a joint power plant, and has sent personnel to begin handling the matter.

Mayor Wu Predicts and Warns – "The Next Three Months Will Be Even More Difficult" – "Stability" Is the Most Needed at Present

Mayor Wu then delivered a speech, stating: "I said earlier that 1947 would be the most difficult year, but the next three months will be even more difficult. In the past, Shanghai experienced gold rushes, student movements, and other incidents. Fortunately, with the assistance of the Municipal Council, the Party Headquarters, and other relevant parties, we were able to get through them safely. We hope that the next few months will also pass smoothly. However, the most needed thing for Shanghai at present is 'stability.' As for 'stability,' the first is to abide by the law and discipline. Otherwise, difficulties in various matters such as transportation, public security, etc., cannot be resolved. The second is to practice austerity. Austerity can increase production and reduce the use of foreign exchange. The trend of extravagance must be overthrown. We hope that the council will assist in establishing a good social atmosphere."

Councilor Zhan Wen, as a representative of the councilors, also expressed that the council should assist the government in stabilizing society. The municipal bureau chiefs attending the conference, from left to right: Wu Kaixian, Zhao Zukang, Shu Ziping, Li a name, Tian Yongqian, Zhu Ping. (Photo by this newspaper)

Policy Address

At the first meeting of the fourth session of the Municipal Council, Mayor Wu reported on the administration of the city. In addition to the written report, the mayor also orally elaborated on important points: Regarding civil affairs: the conscription problem is the most important. The central government has stipulated that 3,000 volunteer soldiers should be recruited, which can be completed by the end of this month. Approximately 120,000 people have applied for exemption from military service, and they are currently being reviewed separately. In order to encourage the city's young men to actively enlist, a consolation association has been jointly organized in each district. Police: Fire prevention work is very important, especially since the communists are inciting citizens to commit arson, which should be guarded against. However, the equipment costs are enormous, which is the most difficult thing. Even so, many improvements have already been made. The police pay is too low, and I have tried many times to find a solution, but without success. I hope the council will assist in formulating a uniform subsidy plan. Society: We have always spared no effort in managing prices, and we have tried our best to keep rice, oil, and food from rising. Most of the pork comes from Jiangbei. We are now doing our best to crack down on extortionate taxes, so the source is gradually becoming smoother. At the same time, we are also negotiating with the Central Trust of China to provide loans to meat merchants, so the price of meat has fallen. The Winter Relief Association is about to be established, and we hope that all sectors will provide assistance. Education: The municipal government is determined to handle the issue of collecting tuition fees, and the fee standards will be openly established by all relevant parties; 5.2 billion yuan has now been collected for scholarships for primary and secondary schools, which will be distributed uniformly by the unified committee; for universities, there will be economic canteens, etc. Finance: The main task now is to consolidate tax revenue. Public Works: The soaring prices of construction materials have made it extremely difficult to carry out projects. The seawall project is progressing smoothly. The Pudong Avenue is of great importance, and we hope to complete it. Public Utilities: There is currently a power crisis. Too little power is used in industry, and too much is used in store displays, which is a huge waste. The truck ferry across the river can be completed in October. Land Administration: Regarding the racecourse issue, because there is a legal basis, formal negotiations cannot be conducted. Only informal consultations are being adopted. The other party has now agreed to first study how much land they need there as a minimum before discussing the matter further. Health: The sanitation problem is the biggest.

Just Discussing Soldiers' Treatment - Suddenly, Women's Cries Heard - Petitioning for Soldiers Occupying Houses Encountered Military Police Harassment and Assault

(Our Report) Yesterday, before the first meeting of the Municipal Council adjourned at noon, while the treatment of soldiers was being hotly debated, a conflict occurred between military police and civilians downstairs, and a pregnant woman was kicked. It turned out that Lin Chunshui and others, representatives of six households living downstairs at No. 18, Nanyongji Lane, Wangzhi Road, came to the Council to petition. They stated that the residents of the building downstairs had a seven-year lease with the landlord, but on the 19th of last month, a soldier named Liu Jimin came and claimed that all the houses downstairs had been taken over by him, forcing them to move out. On the 22nd, Liu occupied the downstairs, forcibly moved the original residents' furniture and objects outside the door, and hung a sign on the door that read "Fourth Warehouse, Engineering Department, United Service Command." This matter has been going on for a month, and the original residents have nowhere to live, so they came to petition, and held a white cloth banner with the words "Soldiers forcibly occupy people's houses, and the common people have no houses to live in. Please uphold justice, Municipal Council." After hearing the news, the Council immediately appointed two councilors, Zhang Xuelian and Shi Zongde, to receive them. At this time, a young military policeman was carrying a large bundle of boots and passed by the area. Seeing the words "Soldiers forcibly occupy people's houses" written on the cloth, he immediately went forward to argue with the petitioners, saying that there were good and bad soldiers and that they should not be generalized, so he accused the petitioning representatives of insult. A conflict broke out immediately, and one of the pregnant women who was petitioning knelt on the ground and pleaded with him. The military policeman kicked her in the abdomen, causing the woman to cry and wail, which immediately aroused public outrage. People pointed out that the military policeman should not hit people, especially not kick a pregnant woman. At that time, several petitioners, together with the duty police officer of the Hongkou Branch, twisted him to the Council to report the incident. The police wanted to take him to the police station, but the military policeman said, "The police can't control the military police." The police officer said, "If you hit someone on the road, you are breaking the law, and this is within my authority." As a result, he was taken to the station to ask for instructions on how to deal with the matter.

Mid-Air SOS from Plane: Passengers Prepared to Parachute - Tokyo Flight a False Alarm

[Our Dispatch] The Northwest Airlines "Shanghai" flight, which departed from America via Tokyo for Shanghai, sent an emergency SOS signal at 5:30 PM yesterday, when it was only 50 miles from Shanghai. The China Aviation Corporation (CAC) received the signal, reporting a fire onboard and a critical situation. The pilot had notified passengers to prepare to parachute and escape, requesting CAC to dispatch a rescue plane immediately.

Upon receiving the message, CAC immediately dispatched aircraft ○46, which took off at once. While in the air, they received another telegram from the "Shanghai" flight, stating that the fire had been extinguished and that everything was alright.

At that time, the CAC airport had already prepared fire trucks and ambulances, anticipating potential accidents during the "Shanghai" flight's landing. At 5:40 PM, the "Shanghai" flight landed slowly and safely. After the passengers hurriedly disembarked, the entire aircraft was thoroughly inspected. Not only was there no trace of fire in the passenger cabin, but the cargo hold was also completely normal.

According to the pilot, Bank, the plane's construction included an automatic fire alarm system in the cargo hold. In case of a fire, a red light in the cockpit would automatically illuminate. When the fire was extinguished, the light would automatically go off. Yesterday, while piloting the Shanghai flight 50 miles from Shanghai, he suddenly noticed the warning light in the front cargo hold illuminate. He immediately used the automatic fire extinguisher. Shortly after, the red light went off, indicating that everything was fine. Just as he was celebrating passing a critical moment, the red light in the rear cargo hold also illuminated. Although he used the automatic fire extinguisher again, it was ineffective. He was then forced to send an SOS signal and fly at a low altitude of 300 feet, notifying the passengers to prepare to parachute and escape. At this critical juncture, the warning light in the rear cargo hold also went off, finally putting his mind at ease. He ultimately landed at Longhua Airport. After repeated research and inspection by CAC mechanical personnel, it was discovered that the false alarm was due to a malfunction in the "automatic fire alarm light" itself, causing it to flicker on and off, while there was actually no fire.

There were eleven passengers aboard the flight to Shanghai yesterday, including Mrs. Zhu Shiming, who boarded the plane when it flew through Tokyo. According to accounts of the time, all the passengers on the plane remained calm. Two Filipino flight attendants, upon learning of the matter, could not help but burst out laughing.

First Shot in News Industry Rectification Campaign: Six Unscrupulous Reporters in the Capital Accused of Soliciting "Entertainment Fees"

[Our Dispatch from Nanjing, 22nd] Amidst the sounds of rectification in the news industry, the capital has taken concrete action to investigate unscrupulous reporters who extorted money under the guise of collecting fees. This matter was revealed in the newspapers on the 20th and has temporarily come to an end on the 22nd. People in the capital's news industry are paying close attention to this matter. It is said that the Reporters Association will soon make a decision, taking it as the first shot in the rectification campaign.

Recently, a resident of Nanjing, Liu Zhennan, committed suicide in front of the house of his enemy Lan Shichang. That afternoon, several reporters went to Lan's house to interview him, claiming that the reports in the newspapers did not match the facts and that Lan needed to provide entertainment fees to the news industry. They extorted 12 million yuan, which was eventually reduced to 3 million yuan. However, another reporter learned of this matter, and the Zongheng News Agency in the city issued a press release on the 19th, detailing the matter. The Central Daily News published it first on the 20th. The leaders of the Capital Reporters Association, the Capital Communications Industry Association, and various newspapers and news agencies in the city attached great importance to the matter and decided to send personnel to

Investigate the Truth

On the afternoon of the 21st, seven major newspapers in the capital sent personnel to jointly investigate, and the truth was gradually revealed. The seven reporters who participated in the joint investigation were Hu Xiaoxian of the Central Daily News, Zhou Xiying of the Peace Daily News, Qian Shaofang of the New People's News, Zhang Gongdu of the Dagang News, Peng Yimin of the Social Daily News, Bai Yaoxi of the Construction Daily News, and Lu Xu of the Nanjing People's News. They were ordered to visit Lan's house on the 21st and invite the complainant to talk to them. They learned the entire story and collectively wrote a report that evening, which was published in various newspapers on the 22nd. According to the

Collective Report

The complainant was Lang Wenzong, a news provider for Zongheng News Agency. He said that a total of six reporters participated in the extortion. According to Lan's second daughter, five of them were Shi Shaofang, a reporter for the social news agency, Xia Qingyun, a reporter for the Construction Daily News, Le Boyuan, a reporter for the Social Daily News, Cao Weiquan, a reporter for the Capital Evening News and the Datong News Agency, and Chen Jishen, a reporter for the Peace Daily News. Another person is still unknown. Lang said: "According to my investigation, Chen was wronged because he was dragged along by others, and I don't think he would do such a thing."

According to the collective report, Cao, Xia, and Le visited Lan Shichang first. Le also invited Lan to talk to him at the Social Daily News, advising Lan to entertain the reporters the next day. The next day, they repeatedly contacted

Lan's Daughter

and classmates, demanding fees for entertaining the reporters and ordering coffee, toast, and dinner. The Lans knew their intentions and thought their character was questionable, so they planned to ignore them. Later, "various inaccurate and distorted reports appeared in various small newspapers." At this time, Lang Wenzong went to interview and learned the truth. Lang claimed to be a representative of the Rectification Committee of the Capital Reporters Association to investigate and obtained the above list, publishing the matter in the newspapers.

Now that the truth of the matter has been clarified, people in the news industry have decided to express their opinions. It is said that the Capital Reporters Association plans to

Expel Membership

of the reporters involved in the incident as a show of rectification. However, Chen Jishen of the Peace Daily News, one of the five mentioned above, applied to the newspaper for temporary resignation when the matter was widely rumored. He said that he was falsely accused this time, and the truth will soon be revealed. To show his self-responsibility, he intends to ask for temporary resignation to await the investigation and resolve the matter according to law, in order to achieve the purpose of rectifying the news industry.

As the reporter was writing this, it was learned that the relevant newspapers had taken

Appropriate Measures

for the unscrupulous news extortion case in the capital. Xia Biaoyun of the Construction Daily News and Sang Boyuan of the Social Daily News have been suspended from their positions by the newspaper authorities and are awaiting legal resolution. The identity of Cao Weiquan, a reporter for the Datong News Agency in the Capital Evening News, is still questionable. The Datong News Agency said that Cao was not a reporter for the agency, while the Capital Evening News said that there was Cao Chao, not Cao Weiquan. Tang Wenlan, president of the Capital Evening News, believes that Lang Wenzong and the newspapers that published the matter on the 22nd slandered the newspaper and should bear legal responsibility. Chen Jishen of the Peace Daily News said that he knew nothing about the extortion. In addition to clarifying his position to the Reporters Association, Chen intends to sue Lang Wenzong for defamation. The Social News Agency believes that Shi Shaofang is a special reporter for the agency, and Shi is outside using the agency's name to swagger around and violate the law. He will be subject to legal sanctions. It is also heard that Cao Weiquan and Le Boyuan also intend to sue Lang Wenzong.

[Our Dispatch from Nanjing, 22nd] In order to implement the rectification of the news industry, the Capital Reporters Association decided to organize a Rectification Committee. Ma Xingye, president of the Central Daily News, was the convener. Ma resigned due to being busy. The Organization Group of the Association was designated to be responsible for convening. The group believed that this matter was related to the reputation of all members. In addition to sending personnel to investigate the truth and correct public perception, they specially formulated reward and complaint methods and announced their implementation to prevent similar incidents from happening again in the future. The methods stipulate:

Any member of this association who is responsible for protecting the reputation of the group and complains about unscrupulous colleagues will be given a certificate of honor by this association after the association's investigation confirms the facts, and it will be awarded in a public ceremony.

Any person from all walks of life who is responsible for complaining about unscrupulous reporters will be given a bonus by this association after the association's investigation confirms the facts. The amount is the sum of three to six months of all salaries and allowances of the person being complained about, depending on the severity of the circumstances. It will be deducted from the service unit of the person being complained about and sent to the association for distribution.

The term "responsible" in the preceding paragraph refers to the complainant listing their real name, address, and position, and signing and sealing the document, detailing the facts of the complaint. If the complaint is made on the basis of personal grievances and is false, the complainant shall also bear legal responsibility.

All complaint letters should be sent to the Organization Group of the Reporters Association, and this association will absolutely keep the secrets of the complainants.

Subei Flood Relief and Work Relief Committee Decides to Distribute Agricultural Loans and Seed Loans

[Our Dispatch from Zhenjiang, 22nd] The Subei Flood Relief and Work Relief Committee held its second meeting yesterday and decided that agricultural loans and seed loans of 15 billion yuan have been approved by the Loan Group of the Four Joint Offices. The Central Bank will provide 10 billion yuan, the Central Cooperative Bank will provide 2 billion yuan, and the China Farmers Bank will provide 3 billion yuan. The loans will be issued separately by the China Farmers Bank and the Cooperative Bank. The meeting passed the outline of the work relief project plan, with a total budget of 150 billion yuan, to be implemented in three phases. The deficit will be covered by funds raised in Shanghai by the Emergency Relief Association.

Kaifeng News Industry Launches Rectification Campaign

[Central News Agency, Kaifeng, 22nd] The Kaifeng News Industry Rectification Campaign Committee held its first executive meeting today and passed the following resolutions on the spot: Publishing announcements in newspapers to ban all colleagues from soliciting donations in any name or form, and notifying all sectors to report violations. Newspapers and news agencies that have been 久 empty shells and have not published or issued news will be legally shut down by the two provincial governments.

Beizhu Self-Defense Force Disarmed: Command Post Sends Personnel to Investigate

[Our Dispatch from Jiangyin, 22nd] The Wuxi Command Post sent staff officer Chen Yuanhao to Cheng to investigate the case of the Beizhu Self-Defense Force being disarmed by the military police. On the 22nd, he went to the countryside with Section Chief Zhang of the County Government to investigate. Because the merchants and residents of Beizhu had gone on strike, they were persuaded to calm down. Fellow villagers from Jiangyin in Shanghai also telegraphed the command post requesting that they be dealt with fairly. (Another telegram) In the southeast villages of Chengdong, the rice planthopper disaster in the late rice crop is severe, and the harvest has been greatly reduced.

"Water Monster" Disappears: Zhenjiang Boats Raise Mast Lights, Sparkling Lights Create a Spectacular Sight

[Our Dispatch from Zhenjiang, 22nd] The case of the "water monster", which aroused suspicion, has occurred four times in Zhenjiang this month. However, after the boatmen repeatedly captured water bandits disguised as "water monsters", the fake water monsters, which had been rampant for a month, have recently subsided slightly. However, the timid boatmen along the river and inland rivers, out of fright, are still mostly vigilant. Recently, large and small boats docked in Zhenjiang, in view of the easy exploitation of dark nights, have prepared an oil mast light to be alert. Therefore, after nightfall, the river bank and the moat are dotted with sparkling lights, creating a spectacular sight. It is heard that the amount of kerosene consumed by each boat is considerable.

Filipino Resident of Taipei, Anthony, Ordered to Find Guarantor and Leave Country by End of Year

[Airmail Dispatch from Taipei, 20th] Anthony, a Filipino resident of Songshan, a suburb of Taipei City, was recently discovered by the police station to have neither a formal passport from his country nor to have completed entry and exit procedures. The Foreign Affairs Section has ordered him to find a guarantor and be deported by the end of the year.

Three Main Offenders in Beijing Temple Arson Case Sentenced to Five Years

[Our Dispatch from Beijing, 21st] In the retrial of the once sensational case of arson at the White Cloud Temple, the sentences of the three main offenders, Xu Xinhe and others, were reduced from life imprisonment to five years. The sentences of the other twelve people were also reduced or they were released. The Military and Administrative Supervision Corps has been effective in "fighting tigers and swatting flies." In the past, special elements relied on their power to bully the Enemy Property Management Bureau, or forcibly buy and refuse to pay. Now, they are automatically clearing up their situations. Zhang Yuzhou, the director of the Blind Children's Academy in the western suburbs of Pingxi, who has a good reputation, was suddenly accused by a blind student, Wu Baipu, in the Supervision Corps of corruption and selling relief flour. Although the student is blind, he knows how to use publicity and has won praise from all walks of life. Bao Guobao, the general manager of the Jibei Electric Power Company, was summoned yesterday for the case of Tu Jingxian, a standing committee member of the Supply Committee of the company, who was suspected of malpractice. He was released on bail pending trial.

Huaifu Highway to Open to Traffic Immediately

[Our Dispatch from Huai'an, 22nd] The Huaifu Highway will open to traffic immediately. The repair work is only remaining on the section from Li'gucun to Yilin, which is about a few miles away from completion.

Boat Capsizes During Opera Performance for Earth Store Bodhisattva's Birthday in Qu County: Tragic Incident Occurs

[News from Hangzhou, 20th] A ferry capsized during an opera performance for the Earth Store Bodhisattva's birthday in Zhangtan, Dongxiang, Qu County, Zhejiang, causing the tragic drowning of thirty to forty people. On that day, women from Nanshandi, Gaoxiang Township, on the opposite bank, flocked to participate in the festivities. However, there was only one small boat at the ferry, and people competed to cross. It carried over sixty people in total. The boat unfortunately sank in the middle of the river, and over sixty people perished in the water, floating up and down the harbor. Apart from about twenty people who were rescued, the rest drowned. The cries on the riverbank shook the heavens. Coffins in Zhangtan Town were bought up, and more had to be purchased from the city.

Xiang River "Water Monster" Alarms People

[Our Dispatch from Hankou, 22nd] Reports of "water monsters" appearing on the Xiang River have been circulating for the past week, alarming residents who are facing what seems like a major disaster. The situation is similar to the rumors in various parts of Jiangsu Province. The water police are busy investigating and suppressing the rumors.

Armed Member of Changzhou Self-Defense Force Shoots and Kills Innocent Civilian, Falsely Claims to Have Killed Water Monster

[News from Changzhou, 20th] Hutangqiao in this county is a large town in the south gate area. There is a Jianguo Grand Theater in the town. Recently, the weather has been fine, and Changzhou Tanhuang opera is being performed. Wang Runhai, an armed member of the town's self-defense force, argued with Zhang Jinda, a villager who was watching the opera, over seats. Wang Runhai was originally a local hooligan. During the enemy puppet period, he served as a secret agent under the traitors Jiang Dingsheng and Yin Liangcheng. After the victory, he managed to become an armed member of the team. However, he remained aggressive and evil, not breaking away from his enemy puppet style. He felt that Zhang Jinda had caused him to lose face by arguing with him over seats. He immediately shouted at his accomplices to drag Zhang Jinda out and beat him. Zhang, fearing for his life, ran across the river. Wang Runhai drew his pistol and shot him dead. He then reported to the district office that he had killed a water monster. Public opinion was outraged. A report was made to the court for inspection. On the 19th, Prosecutor Li Yulong of the court went to the countryside and verified that Zhang had indeed been shot to death. The villagers believed that Zhang Jinda had died unjustly and demanded redress. Prosecutor Li arrested Wang Runhai and detained him pending trial.

Implementation of Large-Scale Suppression in Wu, Yu, Kun, and Tai Counties

[Our Correspondent in Changshu, 22nd] The area along the river here has been taken over by artillery units, and public security has been further consolidated. Large-scale suppression in Wu, Yu, Kun, and Tai counties has been proceeding smoothly. The command headquarters has been established in Ougou Town, east of the city, with four sections: staff, political work, adjutant, and document. Within the suppression zone, land and water transportation are blocked. From 7:00 PM to 6:00 AM the following morning, passage, fishing, gathering for entertainment, and residence are strictly prohibited. Residents of the five townships, including Chou Xing, Su Jian, Ru Bang, and Ji Jing, must carry national identity cards at all times, whether going out or residing, for random inspection.

[Our Correspondent in Huaiyin, 22nd] Yilin Town is the only large town in northern Jiangsu. Agricultural products from the nearby lakes and swamps, as well as salt and cotton from the coast, are all distributed from here. During the war, the area near the town was a stronghold for bandit troops. Now that it has been recovered by the national army, the authorities are determined to build grassroots organizations in this area to ensure normal traffic and solid public security.

Explanation by the Ministry of Justice Regarding Lawsuit Against Prosecutor

[Our Correspondent in Suzhou, 22nd] Regarding the issue of a prosecutor sealing up enemy property and a third party claiming rights and suing the prosecutor, involving the question of who bears the litigation costs, there has been considerable doubt. The Jiangsu High Court submitted the matter to the Ministry of Justice for clarification, which indicated that the prosecutor's litigation costs should be borne as follows: When a prosecutor is sued and appears in court, his seat is the same as that of the defendant's lawyer. The prosecutor can notify the defendant to summon the prosecutor by way of official document instead of having to buy legal stationery.

Regulations of the Jiangsu Provincial Government: Enlistment of Youth Primarily Through Lottery, Supplemented by Voluntary Enrollment

[Our Correspondent in Zhenjiang, 22nd] In order to encourage the youth of the entire province to defend the country and protect their hometowns, the Jiangsu Provincial Government has recently formulated measures and issued orders to all counties and cities to launch a youth enlistment campaign, stipulating that youth enlistment should be based primarily on lottery recruitment, supplemented by voluntary enrollment.

The Last Days of the Arch-Traitor Ye Peng

[Our Correspondent in Nanjing, 17th] Since the victory, great traitors have been arrested and sentenced one by one. The government enforces the law strictly and impartially, which is a most gratifying thing. The arch-traitor Ye Peng, who entrenched himself in Wuhan during the period of occupation, was executed by shooting in Nanjing yesterday morning at 9:30 AM. This arch-traitor met his end on the morning of the 16th anniversary of the "September 18th" National Humiliation Day, which is very heartening and satisfying. At 8:40 AM, the court declared: "The traitor Ye Peng colluded with the enemy, betrayed the country, and plotted to resist this nation. He is sentenced to death." After hearing the verdict, Ye tried to appear calm, repeatedly saying: "It's nothing," "It doesn't matter," only requesting to read the contents of the Chairman's handwritten order. He seemed a little flustered, and his speech was somewhat hesitant. He asked the court if he could say a few words. The court told him to keep it brief.

He said that his death must be due to someone's machinations. He also said: For the sake of his old mother, he did not flee Wuhan and had no choice but to go to Hong Kong. Before going to Hong Kong, he had no thought of things like the "Yan Telegram." Later, he pretended to be "generous" and said: I fought on the front lines, and I am not afraid of death. Everyone has to die, so what is there to fear? Otherwise, I would not be a soldier. Finally, he also said: Although I am ending up this way, I still hope for national unity and the stability of people's lives, and I wish Chairman Chiang good health." At this point, Ye turned around and cast a look at all the listeners, as if seeking sympathy. He issued his last plea before death: Here, there are no outsiders, all "old comrades." I hope everyone will not publicize me as a "traitor," and do not refer to me as a "traitor" in the newspapers! I have no will. My family is all in Shanghai. I hope everyone can sympathize with this request of mine!" At this moment, he seemed to have endless feelings about death.

At 9:10 AM, he was taken to a large truck and driven to the new execution ground at Tianjie Temple outside Zhonghua Gate. He arrived at 9:25 AM. After getting out of the truck, Ye extended his slightly trembling hand and shook hands with the execution supervisor, Chief Luo, and others one by one, repeatedly saying: "There's no way!" "There's no way!" At 9:30 AM, he walked into the execution ground. Just as he was about to turn around and take one last look, the gunshots rang out. The first two shots missed the vital points. The third shot entered from the back and exited from the lower part of the right lung. Ye fell to the ground, his intestines also spilling out, and his whole body spasmed and twitched incessantly. Three minutes later, he breathed his last and died. (Special Correspondent Ding Kuanghua)

Frenzied Purchase of Horse Racing Tickets in Hong Kong, Awaiting the Chance to Gamble a Fortune [Hong Kong Dispatch via Airmail from Our Correspondent, 16th]

Although the weather has been oppressively hot in recent days, more than 300,000 tickets have already been sold for the Autumn Racing Grand Sweepstakes to be drawn on October 11th. Given the record of an estimated 700,000 tickets for the Summer Sweepstakes, people generally expect that this time the number could break one million, and the first prize could reach over 500,000 dollars. The Hong Kong Jockey Club recently shipped in a batch of famous horses from Australia, which were snatched up by horse owners, even more enthusiastically than the general public buying sweepstakes tickets. Happy Valley is stepping up its renovation work in preparation to welcome those who come there to "gamble a fortune."

The Hong Kong police detectives have repeatedly strengthened their forces, and purchased radio patrol cars, and regularly dispatch personnel to patrol the city, to quickly prevent and stop events that violate public order. Hong Kong's public security has significantly improved than before. Recently, in order to effectively protect public security and prevent riots or disruptive group actions from occurring, no expense has been spared in importing various scientific equipment from London, including tear gas. Hong Kong and Chinese police officers have recently added a six-inch wide, ten-inch deep canvas bag to their waists, which contains tear gas and gas masks.

[Our Dispatch] Since the newly appointed County Magistrate Hua Guomo took office, more than thirty people have been laid off. Because they have no way to make a living and because their salaries for June, July, and August have not been paid, they began a hunger strike petition on the 18th and are appealing to all sectors of society.

[Our Dispatch] The six townships including Mazhi have few cotton farmers, but the planting results are very good. Now that the new cotton is on the market, the County Government Cooperative Guidance Office will guide the unified export of American cotton and launch centralized transportation and sales.

Changshu

[Our Dispatch] Zou Weizu, the protagonist of the Yan Gang massacre, was sentenced to death by the District Court. Zou appealed, and the trial is scheduled for the eighth of next month. He has been sent to Suzhou for questioning.

Songjiang

[Our Dispatch] Recently, anthrax has been spreading among draft cattle in the Punan area. Once the disease breaks out, the cattle die within a few hours, and the spread is very rapid. Rural veterinarians cannot treat it. Deaths have been occurring one after another. The Tinglin Agricultural Production and Marketing Cooperative has specially hired experts to go to the countryside for medical consultation and treatment to prevent and control the disease. The Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry has also sent personnel to Songjiang for diagnosis and treatment based on the report.

Chongming

[Our Dispatch] The most dangerous section of the seawall south of the city has been actively repaired and has been completed in stages. It is reported that the Ministry of Water Resources has approved another 1 billion yuan. Once received, all repairs can be completed.

Anhui Education Department Formulates Measures to Deal with Education in Bandit-Affected Areas

[Our Correspondent in Hefei, 22nd] After bandit troops infiltrated western and central Anhui, all public and private schools in the counties were suspended. The Anhui Education Department has specially formulated measures to deal with education in bandit-affected areas, relocating Lihuang Middle School to the territory of Lu'an County, and relocating Taihu Normal School and Tongcheng Women's Normal School to Anqing. Students from bandit areas will be temporarily granted loans by the government. Recruitment committees have been established in Shu, Lu'an, Wu, and Si to recruit faculty and students from private schools, which has already been handled separately. In addition, the high schools in Hefei were disbanded informally when the war situation became tense. Now, all students have been notified to continue registration, and classes are expected to resume next month.

Tianjin Establishes Committee to Award and Assist Impoverished Students, Requiring 390 Million Yuan per Month

[Our Correspondent in Tianjin, 22nd] Tianjin has established the "Committee for the Movement to Award and Assist Outstanding Impoverished Youth," initiated by Mayor Du Jianshi. The number of awards and assistance is stipulated as follows: 2,300 impoverished middle school students, of whom 2,000 will receive awards and assistance for tuition and fees, with 100,000 yuan per student per month, and 300 will receive additional food expenses, with 250,000 yuan per student per month. 400 impoverished college students, with 300,000 yuan per student per month. The total monthly awards and assistance will require 390 million yuan, which will be jointly raised by industry and commerce.

National Day Art Exhibition - Call for Submissions

[Our Correspondent in Nanjing, 22nd] The National Day Art Exhibition of the 36th Year of the Republic of China, organized by the All-China Art Association, is scheduled to be held in Nanjing this year on Double Tenth Day. The association's methods for collecting exhibits are as follows: The content of the submissions includes paintings, sculptures, designs, prints, calligraphy, and epigraphy, etc. Antiques and old paintings will not be accepted. Participating units are divided into individuals and groups. Individuals can send their submissions directly to the association. Groups can collect them and send them to the association together. All submissions will be returned after the exhibition. The submitted works must be fully mounted and intact. The number of submissions is limited to a maximum of three pieces per member and a maximum of two pieces per non-member. If there are too many submissions, limited to the capacity of the exhibition venue, the association may not exhibit all of each person's submissions. The price of the exhibits will be determined by the author. If sold, the association will deduct 10%. If not for sale, it must also be marked. It is planned to select a portion of the works from this exhibition to be sent to Taiwan for exhibition. If you do not wish to participate in the exhibition in Taiwan, please indicate in advance. Submissions must be sent to the association at No. 21 Xiangpu Camp, Nanjing, before the end of September (the date of arrival in Nanjing will be based on the postmark), or sent to the Shanghai Municipal Cultural and Sports Committee at No. 128 Seymour Road, Shanghai, before September 25, for collection by the Shanghai Art Association on behalf of the association. Late arrivals will not be exhibited. For exhibits that are too heavy, you must be responsible for sending them to the association and taking them back after the exhibition.

Lawn Tennis League Ends Successfully - Three Teams Receive Honorary Awards

The city's first team tennis league, organized by the Municipal Sports Association Tennis Committee, ended on Sunday, the 21st. The Physical Education General Association won a trophy after winning 137 points out of 150 matches in ten competitions. The Shanghai Club came in second with 116 points. The competition started on August 17th and was held every Wednesday and Sunday according to the scheduled schedule. There were no delays or other situations. The good spirit was unprecedented in any competition.

The winners of each group in each club include the Shanghai Club's 125 groups and the Physical Education Association's 34 groups. However, among the above five groups, only the Shanghai First Group's Wang Wenzheng and Tang Baojia Group, the Physical Education Association's Ke Nianyi and Wang Jiale's Third Group, and the Shanghai Club's Pan Youyuan and Lu Minjun's Fifth Group have never changed their players. The above three groups should receive the League Honorary Award. As for the group that never lost a game in each group, it is the Physical Education Association's 3rd and 4th groups, but unfortunately, the 4th group had a change of one player. Basketball Committee Passes Basketball Promotion Plan - Selection of Basketball's Top Ten to Be Held at the End of the Month - This Year's League Begins in Early December

The Municipal Sports Association Basketball Committee held its first meeting of this year the day before yesterday, with Chairman Qian Xucang. All Five Proposals Successfully Passed; National Textile Federation Meeting Concludes; Emergency Motion Requests Government Not to Passively Limit Prices

[Our Dispatch] The second general meeting of members of the Textile Federation opened at 10:00 AM yesterday, presided over by Mr. Shu. First, the persons in charge of the engineering and business departments of the Textile Construction Company reported. The current difficulties in textile construction and engineering are summarized as follows: There are not enough parts, and the factories received are mostly Japanese style. Before the war, Japan had 15 million spindles. Currently, only 2.8 million spindles are in operation. There are many surplus parts, so it is hoped that assistance can be obtained from Japan in the future. There is insufficient electricity, so the direct and indirect losses suffered by the factories are large. Regarding raw materials, the textile construction mills mainly spin yarns of 10 counts or more, so the raw materials rely entirely on imported cotton. It is hoped that the import quota can be increased. In terms of business, the main tasks are to supply civilian needs and regulate the prices of yarn and cloth. The methods have been changed repeatedly, but the purpose remains unchanged. Efforts are also being made to obtain foreign exchange. Exports of yarn and cloth have obtained US$4.6 million and £1.6 million. In the future, it is hoped that private yarn factories will cooperate to strengthen foreign sales. After the report, the proposals were discussed and passed, totaling 72 proposals from the meeting affairs, raw materials, production, sales, economic, and administrative groups. All proposals were successfully passed based on the review reports.

Temporary Motions

At this time, the representatives present proposed three urgent temporary motions: Representative Liu Guojun proposed opposing the agricultural market's cotton purchasing plan, believing this action exceeded the responsibilities of the Agricultural Bank and was intended to compete with yarn factories. After discussion, it was passed. Twenty people including Shi Fengxiang, Pan Yangshan, and Wang Zhuyi proposed a motion suggesting the government should insist during peace talks with Japan on revising Japan's industrial level requirements, demanding compensation for spindles, and declaring the right to veto. After discussion, it was passed, and the assembly sent telegrams to the Executive Yuan, Ministry of Economic Affairs, Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and the Political Council. Liu Wensheng proposed a motion suggesting the government should swiftly rescue the economic crisis, promptly reorganize the currency system, and not only implement passive price control policies to avoid affecting production. The motion was passed after deliberation.

After the proposals were discussed, the chairman announced the Assembly Declaration on the spot. The election of the next term of directors and supervisors was still counting votes yesterday. The Price Appraisal Committee of the Commodity Price Appraisal Council Determined the Maximum Price Limit of Flour

Retail Sales Must Not Exceed 159,000 Yuan

[This newspaper's report] The Flour Group of the Shanghai Commodity Price Appraisal Council held the second appraisal meeting at the Social Affairs Bureau at 9:00 a.m. yesterday. Ji Mingzhai, Chief of the Food Section of the Social Affairs Bureau, chaired the meeting and reported that the price of flour was originally strictly limited by the Food Ministry and the China Trust Bureau. Now that the sale of flour has been stopped, the price limit has also been lifted at the same time. It is urgent to determine the price according to the cost and announce it for implementation. Factory representatives and flour merchants expressed their opinions successively. After evaluation by all the representatives present, the factory price was determined to be 153,000 yuan per bag, and the retail price was determined to be no more than 159,000 yuan, according to the previous factory price plus a profit of 4 percent, totaling 6,120 yuan. The appraised price has been approved for implementation by the Director of the Appraisal Committee in accordance with regulations. In addition to reporting to the municipal government for record, the Social Affairs Bureau also immediately announced the matter. If there is any violation of the above appraised price, it will be punished in accordance with the Regulations on Combating Violations of Price Limits and Appraised Prices, and no leniency will be shown.

The representatives attending yesterday also resolved that the Flour Appraisal Committee would hold a meeting every Monday morning at 9:00 a.m.

Social Services

Reader Consultation Legal Interpretation

Disputes Arise from Clearing Debts from Ten Years Ago

An Interlude in the Changing Value of Currency

Dear Editor: A borrowed 200 legal currency from his close friend B in the 26th year of the Republic of China and made a contract. It was stated that it would be paid off within three years, without interest. Now party A wants to repay the money and take back the contract, but party B insists that the legal currency has depreciated and must be calculated according to the proportion of rice prices. In this way, the repayment will be tens of thousands of times more than the original amount, which party A considers too large and cannot afford. Mediation has been ineffective. Now there are several questions, please answer, Is it necessary to calculate the loan of the Republic of China in the 25th year today? Is there any express provision, How is the legal depreciation rate of the legal currency, Is it legal to repay the original 200 yuan with 300,000 yuan today, Are there any precedents in similar disputes in the High Court, and what is the judgment?

[Lawyer Cao Yaxia answers] There is no express provision, but the court may be requested to fairly weigh the increase or decrease in payment in accordance with the provisions of Article 12 of the Supplementary Rules for Handling Civil Litigation after Restoration. The law does not recognize it, and there is no statutory depreciation rate. It is originally legal, but the creditor may sue the court for a ruling if he thinks it is obviously unfair. There is no precedent in the Supreme Court. The disposal of the court varies from place to place. According to what the answerer knows, in Shanghai, there have been precedents of paying back bank deposits before the war at 2,000 times and 4,000 times. However, the Zhejiang High Court ruled in the case of Zhang Shipei's appeal in Jiaxing. Zhang borrowed 250 legal currencies from his friend Zhang Zhaozong in the 28th year of the Republic of China. It was impossible to recover the money during the war. After the victory of the Anti-Japanese War, after repeated negotiations, the opinions of the parties were not close, resulting in litigation. Initially, the local court ruled that the defendant should repay 1,000 times. The plaintiff refused to accept the appeal and was sentenced to pay 10,000 times.
